  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_6ea6641f-40cc-4a23-bdf3-ced679794637'
      });
    }

  <span id="freeText11841023475211536724" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>The Billionaire Boys Club is a secret society of six men who have vowed success—at any cost. Not all of them are old money, but all of them are incredibly wealthy. They’re just not always as successful when it comes to love…</i>
</b><br /> <br />Real-estate tycoon Hunter Buchanan has a dark past that’s left him scarred and living as a recluse on his family’s palatial estate. Hunter is ready to give up on love—until he spots an enigmatic red-haired beauty and comes up with an elaborate scheme to meet her.<br /> <br />Gretchen Petty is in need of a paycheck—and a change. So when a job opportunity in an upstate New York mansion pops up she accepts. And while she can overlook the oddities of her new job, she can’t ignore her new boss’s delectable body—or his barely leashed temper.<br /> <br />Hunter’s afraid his plan might be unraveling before it’s truly begun, but Gretchen is about to show him that life can be full of surprises…</span>

  <span id="freeText5940738399413826066" style="display:none"><br><blockquote>
  <b>Dark Broody Cranky Male …… CHECK <br>Sexy and Scarred ……. CHECK ( some women find scars sexy) <br>Billionaire…….. CHECK <br>Virgin Hero…… CHECK<br><br>WHAT….. <br><br>He is a virgin.... <br>Say what?? </b>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer672103750" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14618256335442590403">I am about to go on a gush-fest right now, as I absolutely adore this book! It has been awhile since I have been captivated by a read, and this story did it. Hunter Buchannon is a man who was such a pleasant surprise to me, I fell in hard core love with him..I truly did!<br/><br/>This book is the second in the series; "The Billionaire Boys Club." Even though this is the second book, I do feel it can be read as a stand alone, although Book one was extremely enjoyable as well. "Beauty and the Billionaire" h</span>
  <span id="freeText14618256335442590403" style="display:none">I am about to go on a gush-fest right now, as I absolutely adore this book! It has been awhile since I have been captivated by a read, and this story did it. Hunter Buchannon is a man who was such a pleasant surprise to me, I fell in hard core love with him..I truly did!<br /><br />This book is the second in the series; "The Billionaire Boys Club." Even though this is the second book, I do feel it can be read as a stand alone, although Book one was extremely enjoyable as well. "Beauty and the Billionaire" has the "Beauty and the Beast" theme that a lot of us readers love. I can honestly say that it has been awhile since I have read a book with this theme that I have enjoyed so much. This story will be one of my top faves of all time when it comes to the "beast" theme. Let me tell you...Mr. Hunter Buchannon..may look like a monster because of his scars...but in no way is he one. This guy will hold you entrhralled from beginning to end. I seriously felt so much for him. He was gruff yes, but underneath that hard exterior was a man that had so many soft layers he was amazing! He is kind, thoughtful, and feels like he doesn't deserve happiness because of how he looks. He hides himself away from the world, as he has been rejected and gawked at so many times that he would just rather be alone. He does have his friends that he met in College. These are the Billionaires that he has formed a private club with. There are six of them, and they have taken a vow to be successful no matter what they have to do. They rely on each other to help themselves out, and they are all handsome and filthy rich. (well, besides Hunter..he's rich but most would say he wasn't handsome..)Unfortunately, none of them are very lucky in love...<br /><br />When Hunter comes across a woman named; Gretchen Petty, he is held captivated by her. She has the bright red hair, and she is vibrant and unique. He overhears her talk about how she wishes she could find a good man, and how looks do not matter to her. Even though Hunter knows in his heart that no one would be able to over look him..he decides he needs to formulate a plan to get to know this woman who has caught his attention. Gretchen is a "ghost writer" and Hunter uses her profession to lure her in to his mansion to stay there for a month. Gretchen is tempted by the huge amount of money she is offered, even though there are a few very strange conditions about the job.<br /><br />I loved Gretchen! She was just such a neat heroine..so full of life,love, and laughter! She was perfect for Hunter, and thankfully she had so much determination when it came to the recluse! Hunter was innocent and naive in so many ways (yes, sex was one of the major ones!) and she took it upon herself to want to show him how to live! As the two of them grow closer, I fell in love more and more! I can't say enough of how much I enjoyed their dance to falling in love. This will go down as one of my favorite love stories of all time. Not all readers may be as excited about this story as I was; but for me...I just can't say enough good about it!<br /><br />The sex between this couple...holy smoly...it was beyond HOT! Hunter may have gotten a late start; but when he finally does the deed..this guy is a demon in bed! Phew!!! I love his enthusiasum and his intensity! There is quite a bit of sex in this installment; but I wasn't complaining!! IT was all around great sex, and very well written. No trashiness in the least. It was erotic,passionate, and I loved every word...At one point I was reading a scene (them against a wall!) in the grocery store, and I had to stop as I was sure my face was beat red, and everyone would know that I was reading a dirty scene! LMAO That is a true story people!!! <br /><br />Jessica Clare is fast becoming a top fave author of mine! I am in love with this series. If I have one book recommendation of the year so far...it would be this one! If "Beauty and the Beast" is something that you have always enjoyed..then please...give this one a chance. You will fall in love with Hunter...truly you will! He is such a pleasant surprise! I was sad to have the story end!</span>

Until she meets her new boss and everything changes. <br>Hunter knows he wants her, but he gave up love and doesn’t believe anyone would want him that way. But that’s the thing about Gretchen, she is used to see inside of people and knows how deep beauty can go. If only Hunter would let her watch closely… <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388683472i/7901653.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars. <br> <b>Storyline: </b> Not original. I mean, the “beauty and h beast” plot is everything but new. Despite being predictable, everyone likes this type of story and we love to read it, even knowing exactly what’s going to happen. <br> <b>Writing Style: </b> First person. Pretty well written and kind of addictive. It seemed like I was in the middle of a modern fairy-tale and I loved every second of it. <br> <b>Character Development: </b> Gretchen is a pretty good heroine. Not to mention, she’s a writer. (I love writers for some reason!). <br>Hunter, despite some annoyances, it’s pretty good either and I liked him a lot. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot. <br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16324331614998180508" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1642965118" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1642965118" />
    <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read"><img alt="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1504717217p2/3068938.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1642965118?book_show_action=true">May 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read">Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=mo-money-mo-problems">mo-money-mo-problems</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=i-m-broken">i-m-broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=thumbs-up-leading-lady">thumbs-up-leading-lady</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=too-hot-for-tv">too-hot-for-tv</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1642965118" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17456996137231987160"><br/><b>***4.25 Stars***</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I don't find you ugly, Hunter. No one who knew you could. If anything, I'm grateful that you have these scars, because they saved you for me - for this moment in time. And that's a little selfish of me, isn't it? And yet I can't help but feel that way."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>This was quite the delicious slow build of sexual tension and trepidation. A fiesty, sarcastic and larger than life redhead paired with a scarred, broody loner. I ate this book up with a voracious appetite. <br/><br/>Hunter spot</span>
  <span id="freeText17456996137231987160" style="display:none"><br /><b>***4.25 Stars***</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I don't find you ugly, Hunter. No one who knew you could. If anything, I'm grateful that you have these scars, because they saved you for me - for this moment in time. And that's a little selfish of me, isn't it? And yet I can't help but feel that way."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />This was quite the delicious slow build of sexual tension and trepidation. A fiesty, sarcastic and larger than life redhead paired with a scarred, broody loner. I ate this book up with a voracious appetite. <br /><br />Hunter spotted Gretchen by accident, but immediately was intrigued by her quirky and outgoing personality. And with more money than he knows what to do with, he concocts a plan to get her to his sprawling mansion so he can get to know her and possibly strike up a friendship. <br /><br />Gretchen is offered a perfect timing, too good to be true job offer...move into a mansion, read through hundreds of love letters from the old inhabitants and write a book based on their tale. Gretchen jumps at the chance for adventure...but she wasn't expecting to find Hunter Buchanan there. A sad and lonely man who hides in the shadows because of his scars. <br /><br />Gretchen is beyond intrigued by the man. Yes, the scars are jarring at first, but she can easily see past them to the man underneath. A man who hides from the world, a man who has never known a woman's touch, a man who doesn't see beauty in himself, but tends to his garden with care and reverence, a man who hides behind cold gruffness to keep people at a distance in order to protect himself. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I saw a man who isolates himself because he's worried about making other people uncomfortable. I saw a man who doesn't leave his house very often, but makes sure that the staff are well paid. I saw a man who works all day tirelessly and tends to roses because he enjoys their beauty. I saw man who expects perfection in himself but is okay with others treating him like dirt. I see a man who shuts out the world because he's so afraid of getting hurt again."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />But Gretchen will not be deterred...she'll break him out of his shell, show him that he is desired and teach him how to come out of the shadows. <br /><br />The depth of Hunter's loneliness broke my heart. He was so broken down by people's reactions to him. He was terrified of rejection, yet aching for a connection. Watching him open up to Gretchen melted my heart. Seeing him stumble through simple conversation, fumble at flirting and tremble with nervousness when it came to his sexual desires made him unbelievably endearing. He held on with both hands to the connection he shared with Gretchen, but he dared not hope that it would last. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I'm a practical man. I never thought to have a woman in my life, ever. I thought my face would turn off any woman worth having. I never thought I would be lucky enough to meet someone like you. I have no illusions as to what this means to you, but for me, it is the world."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I just want you to know that it's not you. It's me. It's all me, and if I push you away it's because I don't know how to pull you close."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />This book was just a great combination of so many elements...emotion, humor, healing, desire and love. I loved Gretchen's humor and openness...she refused to let Hunter hide, but knew when to retreat and went to give him the push that he needed. Watching Hunter step out of his self imposed exile and show his vulnerabilities to Gretchen gave me those swoony stomach flutters that I live for. However, neither Gretchen nor Hunter were perfect, and mistakes are made along the way, but no matter what it was clear that they belonged together. <br /><br />I'm a sucker for Beauty and the Beast-esque books, and this one hit on all the things that I love. Jessica Clare's effortless writing continues to make this an addicting series that I just can't seem to put down. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17456996137231987160" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_592455656" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/592455656" />
    <a title="MARQUETTA" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1436213-marquetta"><img alt="MARQUETTA" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1502287573p2/1436213.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/592455656?book_show_action=true">Apr 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MARQUETTA" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MARQUETTA" href="/user/show/1436213-marquetta">MARQUETTA</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer592455656" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12170191318367003973">I am in love with this series. I was hesitant to read the first book because it had 'billionaire' in the title and I kind of sworn off Billionaire books. But this series is so different from other Billionaire books out there. I'm so happy that I gave this series a chance.<br/><br/>We met Hunter in the first book. He lives a pretty solitary life thanks to his scarred face. In book 1, when he spies on Gretchen and Bronte, he is immediately taken with Gretchen. He hears her say that she doesn't care about a </span>
  <span id="freeText12170191318367003973" style="display:none">I am in love with this series. I was hesitant to read the first book because it had 'billionaire' in the title and I kind of sworn off Billionaire books. But this series is so different from other Billionaire books out there. I'm so happy that I gave this series a chance.<br /><br />We met Hunter in the first book. He lives a pretty solitary life thanks to his scarred face. In book 1, when he spies on Gretchen and Bronte, he is immediately taken with Gretchen. He hears her say that she doesn't care about a man's looks and he figures that if she truly means that, Gretchen could be the woman for him. Hunter finds out everything he can about Gretchen and lures her to his house under false pretenses. I know this sounds creepy but it's really not. At least, I didn't think it was creepy.<br /><br />Gretchen is intrigued by the writing job that miraculously landed in her lap. When she arrives at Hunter's home, she's taken aback by how stark it is. His butler is not very cooperative and there aren't a bunch of servants running around. When Gretchen finally meets Hunter, it's not under the best circumstances and when she tries to apologize, she keeps making the situation worse. Gretchen slowly brings Hunter out of his shell and when she sees his face, she understands why he lives such a solitary life. Gretchen is intrigued by Hunter and wants to get to know him better, a lot better.<br /><br />I love the Beauty and the Beast spin of Beauty and the Billionaire. When I learned that Hunter was a virgin, I was immediately sold. Gotta love those virgin heroes. Hunter's virginity was handled realistically. He's no stud in the bed, he gets too excited a couple of times and pretty much doesn't know what to do. Gretchen's patience with him was sweet and sexy. She wasn't concerned about Hunter's looks. She wanted to be with him despite his looks.<br /><br />Hunter's wounds are not just on his face. Because of his scars he doesn't trust that someone like Gretchen would like him for him. Hunter and Gretchen's perfect life unravels when outside forces invade their cozy environment. The journey to an HEA is not an easy road for Gretchen and Hunter. Hunter has to learn to trust and Gretchen has to forgive Hunter.<br /><br />Beauty and the Billionaire is a great installment in this series. I loved Hunter and Gretchen. They are a great couple and loved their journey together. Can't wait to read the next book!<br /><br />If you haven't started reading this series yet, I highly recommend you do.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12170191318367003973" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText1543605166376474835" style="display:none"><b>Gretchen Petty</b><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426390693i/14010303.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Hunter Buchanan</b><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426390693i/14010304._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Here's my review to my wonderful and faithful readers :D!!<br><br>So Gretchen has money problems and she needs funding, fortunately a guy -cough- HUNTER BUCHANAN -cough- has the means to help her with his cha-ching ;)..<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398915007ra/9481977.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When they first meet... LMAO<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426390693ra/14010305.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As their love flowers..no pun intended (you'll catch that later)<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398334402ra/9401792.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The mutual acceptance and understanding of one another...<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426390821ra/14010315.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Party :|....<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426390693ra/14010308.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All those bouquets :D!!!....<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393547990ra/8729945.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>From an early age we are taught to never judge a person based on what they do or don't have physically. Easier said then done though, right? Yeah. <br>After reading this book which is ultimately a spicier remake of a classic tale of finding love and overcoming insecurities that are brought out by the cruel nature of human beings, I have to say that it has served as a good reminder of how often people are quick to judge a person before knowing the demons that may lie beneath. <br><br>If you're looking for an out of the ball park new and exciting book, this may not be the stunner book you're looking for, but I encourage everyone to put this on their reading list, ESPECIALLY if you're in a reading slump and are looking to ease your way back into the world of reading, but I also recommend this book because it is always valuable to learn a lesson in love while readers build or restructure their "book army". :) <br><br>This book emphasizes the unarguable fact that true love is <b>never</b> ugly, something that nobody should forget &lt;3<br><br>As is my sign off, thanks again to my wonderful readers.. until next time &lt;3<br><br>Tierra</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/969756882" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/969756882?book_show_action=true">Jun 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer969756882" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4802660093324869315"><b>5 Heart Warming “Beauty and the Beast” STARS</b><br/> <br/><b>OH.MY.GOSH! If you love the story of Beauty and the Beast then this book is for you!!!! It’s SUPER SUPER SUPER CUTE!!!!</b><br/> <br/>You have the scared Hero, Hunter. He has scars all over his face, his torso and he’s also missing a finger! Don’t you feel for him? Because he’s so scared, Hunter is recluse, stays in his mansion and hardly gets out, but he’s also very lonely.<br/> <br/>Gretchen is a beauty, but a broke one. She’s a writer and she’s writes books she doesn’t li</span>
  <span id="freeText4802660093324869315" style="display:none"><b>5 Heart Warming “Beauty and the Beast” STARS</b><br> <br><b>OH.MY.GOSH! If you love the story of Beauty and the Beast then this book is for you!!!! It’s SUPER SUPER SUPER CUTE!!!!</b><br> <br>You have the scared Hero, Hunter. He has scars all over his face, his torso and he’s also missing a finger! Don’t you feel for him? Because he’s so scared, Hunter is recluse, stays in his mansion and hardly gets out, but he’s also very lonely.<br> <br>Gretchen is a beauty, but a broke one. She’s a writer and she’s writes books she doesn’t like, but she does it for the pay check. When a publishing company offers her a job to write a book for lots of money, it’s too hard to pass up. However, she must write a book where her references are located and it’s in a mansion.<br> <br>Wait for it….<br> <br>At Hunter’s mansion! Because Hunter set up the publishing company to get to know Gretchen better.<br> <br><b>Review</b><br> <br>I’m starting to really like this series. This one just takes the cake on cuteness factor. I couldn’t get over the storyline and I wanted to gobble ever y page. The heart of the story lies within Hunter. He’s so damaged because of his appearance, as he should because he lets us know how people cringe when they see him.<br> <br>I LOVE HUNTER!!!! He’s so venerable, adorable, awkward and crazy sexy at the same time. Since he was scared at a young age, so he doesn’t have much experience with women and when he’s around Gretchen, he’s put off and very timid.<br> <br>Gretchen is sassy and has a very cute personality. I wouldn’t say she’s super strong character, but just a fun-loving, I-want-to-be-her-friend kind of character. She tries to banter with Hunter to get him to loosen up and it’s really sweet to read.<br><br>Hunter is very attracted to Gretchen and longs for her but because of his appearance he doesn’t attempt to get closer to Gretchen, he’s perfectly fine just having her around. Gretchen is intrigued by Hunter and wants to purse a friendship with him, but Hunter doesn’t make it easy for her.<br> <br>I really like Beauty and the Billionaire because of how Jessica Clare set up her characters. She created a hero that was just so interesting and loving to read I was just immersed. This story mirrors a lot like the Beauty and Beast storyline, but it’s not an exact plot. I love this because Beauty and the Billionaire is just a new modern twist from a classic fairy tale.<br> <br>I could have ready this over and over . I recommend! <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17561022.Stranded_with_a_Billionaire__Billionaire_Boys_Club___1_" title="Stranded with a Billionaire (Billionaire Boys Club, #1) by Jessica Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1362603720s/17561022.jpg" alt="Stranded with a Billionaire (Billionaire Boys Club, #1) by Jessica Clare" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578568258" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0425269078/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=0425269078&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=F4XBBPWM5WDONSPO" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17825218.Beauty_and_the_Billionaire__Billionaire_Boys_Club___2_" title="Beauty and the Billionaire (Billionaire Boys Club, #2) by Jessica Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1366125283s/17825218.jpg" alt="Beauty and the Billionaire (Billionaire Boys Club, #2) by Jessica Clare" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_604089827" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/604089827" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/604089827?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer604089827" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17428614501486692603">Beauty and the Billionaire is the second installment of the Billionaire Boys Club and the story of Hunter Buchanan & Gretchen Petty.<br/><br/>We met these two in Stranded, Gretchen was the quirky roommate with the hairless cat and Hunter was the deeply scarred recluse man who in a moment of overhearing Gretchen's words knows he has to have her.<br/><br/>Hunter has money at his disposal and he plans on using it to lure Gretchen in with the hopes that he can get to know her - even love her. But he knows that she will</span>
  <span id="freeText17428614501486692603" style="display:none">Beauty and the Billionaire is the second installment of the Billionaire Boys Club and the story of Hunter Buchanan &amp; Gretchen Petty.<br><br>We met these two in Stranded, Gretchen was the quirky roommate with the hairless cat and Hunter was the deeply scarred recluse man who in a moment of overhearing Gretchen's words knows he has to have her.<br><br>Hunter has money at his disposal and he plans on using it to lure Gretchen in with the hopes that he can get to know her - even love her. But he knows that she will never look past his disfiguring scars, but he still craves her to be near him, even if she will never return the feelings.<br><br>But Gretchen finds herself drawn into the man, she is able to see beyond his scars to something that is far deeper within. She sees the scared broken boy that suffered all those years ago and the man that is still trying to shield himself from the hurt those visual reminders bring out.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419693i/832396.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But as Hunter finds himself falling in love with her, his lack of experience shows through. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes ladies, the man is a virgin <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>...and this made his story something so much more raw and vulnerable. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419693i/832397.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419693ra/832398.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Hunter fights with his need to hide away and the urges to use his money and power throughout this story. Hunter and Gretchen struggle with trust; he can't seem to understand that a woman could truly love him with a body mangled with such horrific reminders. But when Gretchen discovers that Hunter has set everything in motion she struggles with feeling betrayed.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419693i/832399.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am not sure what it is about men with scars that makes me fall deeper. Without the ability to rely solely on the author's ability to clearly state just how good-looking or hot the male lead is - you are stuck focusing on actions and for me it just hits me in the heart just right. And I mean, we are all suckers for the fairy tales right? <br><br>Between the heartache of his transformation and the heated sexual encounters this was a wonderful read and was a great installment in this series - of the two, this one is my favorite of the group and I am not sure if the other 3 will surpass this one for me. There were some pretty intense sexual situations that were bordering on innocent, but felt a little more erotic than they were because of the situation that Hunter was faced with. <br><br>A great series read for those who like their alpha males ridiculously rich and every bit broken. Audrey &amp; Reese's story is up next and I have a feeling he will be the bad boy we will love to hate.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <a title="Susan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/739211-susan"><img alt="Susan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1335133091p2/739211.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/750835263?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Susan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Susan" href="/user/show/739211-susan">Susan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer750835263" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8754172298775847222"><br/>Contemporary take on Beauty and the Beast...the "beast" being an injury-mutilated/scarred billionaire. <br/><br/>It's been a bit since I've read a het romance book and quite frankly, I think just because the sheer volume of options and choices that are produced out there, it's really hard to find the good ones. This was an ok read...it's hella cheesy and for being a contemporary book, I'm disappointed at how...unrealistic so much of it is. Suspension of reality and overlooking lame details is required. <br/><br/>Th</span>
  <span id="freeText8754172298775847222" style="display:none"><br />Contemporary take on Beauty and the Beast...the "beast" being an injury-mutilated/scarred billionaire. <br /><br />It's been a bit since I've read a het romance book and quite frankly, I think just because the sheer volume of options and choices that are produced out there, it's really hard to find the good ones. This was an ok read...it's hella cheesy and for being a contemporary book, I'm disappointed at how...unrealistic so much of it is. Suspension of reality and overlooking lame details is required. <br /><br />That being said, I think one thing the book does well is tell the fairy tale...and sometimes I just want to believe a strapped-for-cash ghost writer can live in Soho and fall in love with a billionaire virgin who looks like a "monster'. <br /><br />There are some hot and sensual scenes but the problem is it's the same thing over and over...no variety. I kinda love how my M/M books have guys doing each other every which way, facing all directions, and in places and positions galore. The sex in this one started to get boring...<br /><br />All in all, a quick decent read. But, I really need a book w/ 2 strapping alpha males getting it on like donkey kong next...may need to reread <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6235223.Grey_s_Awakening__Cabin_Fever___2_" title="Grey's Awakening (Cabin Fever, #2) by Cameron Dane" rel="nofollow noopener">Grey's Awakening</a> or one of my Cut &amp; Run books. :)<br /><br />Thanks to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3173295.Heidi_Cullinan" title="Heidi Cullinan" rel="nofollow noopener">Heidi Cullinan</a> and Tina Miz for the buddy read via twitter! :)</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8584800586774733717"><b>For my "Fellow Safety gang" this book is safe: No OW/OM apart form heroine's friend is in love with her, but nothing happened between them</b><br/><br/>Overall i enjoyed this romance with all the grumpy butler and some very funny comic scenes that made me laugh a lot!<br/><br/><b>Hero:</b> was scarred on his face and because of that he did not believe that someone would "love him" for who he is and that made him a loner hiding in his big house, isolating himself from outside world which ultimately made him very moody and roug</span>
  <span id="freeText8584800586774733717" style="display:none"><b>For my "Fellow Safety gang" this book is safe: No OW/OM apart form heroine's friend is in love with her, but nothing happened between them</b><br /><br />Overall i enjoyed this romance with all the grumpy butler and some very funny comic scenes that made me laugh a lot!<br /><br /><b>Hero:</b> was scarred on his face and because of that he did not believe that someone would "love him" for who he is and that made him a loner hiding in his big house, isolating himself from outside world which ultimately made him very moody and rough around the edges! He likes flowers and even have a full garden of plans and take care of them himself. I liked that quality about him..it added extra dimension to his character development, thus, I wish there was more in depth emotional development around his character! At times I found myself frustrated with him for "not going after what he wants" YES the reader knows the reasons behind: His inability to communicate and lack of faith in another human being for liking him or love him for himself, but at times I felt that the "chase" was one sided and heroine was doing most of the working on their relationship! I guess, its down to my personal tastes..I like my heroes to be more on the possessive side, but that's not to say the hero was not appealing! He was very unique in his own way by way of bringing roses to the heroines room every day which was very romantic and endearing!<br /><br /><b>Heroine:</b> was a very likable character that I immediately admired for her bravery in pursuing the hero no matter what his rejection was! She was very bold and went after what she wanted which was exactly what the hero needed at the time! Having said hat, there were moments where I wanted "the Hero" to step up and be the man that heroine deserves! She never give up on him and thought of his scars as sexy..so I REALLY wanted him to make more initiatives! Alas, it was still a very sweet and not to heavy on the plot read! if you like inexperienced Hero and entire focus on the couples relationship development like I like then you will definitely like this book!</span>

<div id="review_606888731" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/606888731" />
    <a title="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3758447-vikki-squee-lite"><img alt="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368215503p2/3758447.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/606888731?book_show_action=true">May 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" href="/user/show/3758447-vikki-squee-lite">Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer606888731" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8631725235006644334">I LOVED this book. <br/><br/>Ever since we met Gretchen in the first book, I knew she was my kind of heroine. Smart, spunky, and irreverent. She certainly set the tone for the whole book. <br/><br/>Gretchen is a ghost writer who hates her job. She writes crap. The tile of the novel she is working on is <i> Astronout Bill and the Space Vixens of Dark Planet </i> . Is it any wonder she can't seem to make her deadline? So, when she's offered an interesting and lucrative job to write a novel based on a series of Victorian era</span>
  <span id="freeText8631725235006644334" style="display:none">I LOVED this book. <br /><br />Ever since we met Gretchen in the first book, I knew she was my kind of heroine. Smart, spunky, and irreverent. She certainly set the tone for the whole book. <br /><br />Gretchen is a ghost writer who hates her job. She writes crap. The tile of the novel she is working on is <i> Astronout Bill and the Space Vixens of Dark Planet </i> . Is it any wonder she can't seem to make her deadline? So, when she's offered an interesting and lucrative job to write a novel based on a series of Victorian era letters, even though she has to live in a strangers house, she takes it. <br /><br />I adored Gretchen and Hunter's dance around each other. Hunter was so different than your usual Billianare fare. He is more than just reclusive - he's sure that no woman, no person could look beyond his scars to the man beneath. <br /><br /><i> <b> "I dont find you ugly Hunter. No one who knows you could. .....If anything, I'm grateful that you have these scars, because they saved you for me - for this moment in time." </b> </i> <br /><br /><br />Gretchen is tailor made for Hunter. She doesn't like perfect alpha guys, and is drawn to the lonely mysterious man she sees in Hunter. Hunter turns out to be a deeply romantic, passionate man that is the perfect complement to Gretchen in every way. <br /><br />And boy, when they finally get together...talk about chemistry. They were off the charts. <br /><br />I think my only complaint was that this was FAR from an original storyline (as evidenced by even the title, this one was recycled from way back). However, it was so well executed, it is hard to care. <br /><br />Overall, it was fantasticly funny, sweet, romantic, and steamy. Definitely a recommended read. <br /><br /><br /></span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2970479346020895176"><b>Everyone has a hard time getting out of the way of their own self esteem, don't they?</b><br/><br/>And sometimes we're all jerks because of that little self esteem issue, right?<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1487560880ra/22026273.gif' width='245' height='175' alt='kind of a dick' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>This is the perfect case of self esteems getting in the way. Nothing shocking there, this is a beauty and the beast trope. <br/><br/><b>NOTE: read for New Years 2017 Reading Challenge, Contemporary Romance category. </b><br/><br/><b>Setting / Time / Genre:</b> Current, New York<br/><br/><b>Series:</b> Yes. This is the second and it was way more interesting than the first. Nice diverti</span>
  <span id="freeText2970479346020895176" style="display:none"><b>Everyone has a hard time getting out of the way of their own self esteem, don't they?</b><br><br>And sometimes we're all jerks because of that little self esteem issue, right?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1487560880ra/22026273.gif" width="245" height="175" alt="kind of a dick" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This is the perfect case of self esteems getting in the way. Nothing shocking there, this is a beauty and the beast trope. <br><br><b>NOTE: read for New Years 2017 Reading Challenge, Contemporary Romance category. </b><br><br><b>Setting / Time / Genre:</b> Current, New York<br><br><b>Series:</b> Yes. This is the second and it was way more interesting than the first. Nice diverting reads/<br><br><b>Sexy times:</b>Yep. Plenty. We've got a virgin hero. Time to work that. <br><br><b>Plan on reading more by the author: </b> Here and there, yes. <br><br><b>Synopsis</b> Virgin hero. Scarred dude. Billionaire. Recluse. Red headed heroine with a heart shaped ass (apparently). Saucy and spicy. Hero manipulates her in to ghost writing and epistolary novel. Love is found, she finds out he's doing all the manipulation. Shit hits the fan. And then it doesn't. And then we end up doing the super happy dance for the two characters. Now, I'm simplifying here, you get that, right? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1487560880ra/22026274.gif" width="245" height="160" alt="happy" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Heroine:</b> Gretchen. Oohhhh I mostly dug her attitude. Like any awkward thing that she could say, she did say. Now, there were times she needed to work on speaking out in defense of the hero and in defense of herself, but she doubts herself and her worth and so she doesn't. This does not portend well. She spends a lot of time in yoga pants. Like it's mentioned 10 plus times. At least. Again, I respect her for this. I love my yoga pants. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448560259ra/17159142.gif" width="400" height="203" alt="sweat pants" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Hero:</b> Typical billionaire type. But, he's a total recluse. And he has some serious issues. About himself physically and about why someone would want him. He's loving and at the same time unloving and even unloveable. <br><br><b>Why it did or didn't work for me:</b> It worked. It was interesting enough to keep my focus and I cared enough about the characters to keep listening. Solid. That's how I would describe it. <br><br>Signed, <br><b>
  <i>Good work, Ms. Clare. Keep it up. </i>
</b><br><br><b>See ya!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1487560880ra/22026275.gif" width="400" height="215" alt="peace" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="2970479346020895176" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1811160977" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1811160977" />
    <a title="Ivy Deluca" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7751086-ivy-deluca"><img alt="Ivy Deluca" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1573265162p2/7751086.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1811160977?book_show_action=true">Nov 13, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ivy Deluca" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ivy Deluca" href="/user/show/7751086-ivy-deluca">Ivy Deluca</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18242048-beauty-and-the-billionaire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7751086-ivy-deluca?shelf=billionaires">billionaires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7751086-ivy-deluca?shelf=beauty-and-the-beast">beauty-and-the-beast</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7751086-ivy-deluca?shelf=scarred-hero">scarred-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1811160977" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10222906669370114392">4.5 stars<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434745281i/15258398.png' width='400' height='150' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>-Cleaning out my kindle, and realizing that I had the novella follow up to this as an ARC to read compelled me to dig around the Mountain (aka my TBR pile) and I discovered that I had held onto this book, for reasons unknown to me. Boy was I missing out. Gretchen and Hunter’s touching love story was an absolute treat and considering the crappy week I’ve had, it absolutely hit the spot.<br/><br/>-With a title like Beauty and the Billionaire, I don’t think a recap’s that necessary but here goes - H</span>
  <span id="freeText10222906669370114392" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434745281i/15258398.png" width="400" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>-Cleaning out my kindle, and realizing that I had the novella follow up to this as an ARC to read compelled me to dig around the Mountain (aka my TBR pile) and I discovered that I had held onto this book, for reasons unknown to me. Boy was I missing out. Gretchen and Hunter’s touching love story was an absolute treat and considering the crappy week I’ve had, it absolutely hit the spot.<br><br>-With a title like Beauty and the Billionaire, I don’t think a recap’s that necessary but here goes - Hunter sees Gretchen from a far and decides that he must find a way to meet her and spend time with her. Gretchen’s a ghostwriter who’s struggling to find any inspiration in the series she’s currently writing, she jumps at a chance to examine some letters and write a story about them. Yes, take the general structure of the fairy tale, add in some good humor, hot sex and lots of roses, and romance happens.<br><br>-Hunter’s your prototypical wounded hero, damaged inside and out. His inner monologue is tortured. He’s socially awkward and a deeply lonely man. So of course, I fell madly in love with him. His yearning and love for Gretchen made every bit of my romantic feels like up like a Christmas tree. Yes, in his pain and inability to understand how anyone could want to be with him and his scars, I just want to hug him. With my mouth.<br><br>-Gretchen is the perfect antidote for Hunter. She sees beyond his scars, and is drawn to the man beneath it all. She’s not perfect, she’s a bit of a procrastinator, unsure at times, but for the most part, she refuses to let him hide himself from her and I absolutely adored her.<br><br>-So, of course with this angsty type read, there’s questionable choices, misunderstandings and I could point to frustrations of it. And lord have mercy, Gretchen’s sister Daphne is still as annoying as I’ve ever found her in other Jessica Clare Billionaire books she’s been featured in. That said, Gretchen and Hunter’s romance is sexy, emotional and enjoyable enough that I could gloss over those annoying moments and just love them. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434745281i/15258399.png" width="400" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>4.5 stars<br>I truly enjoyed Beauty and the Billionaire. A treat I denied myself for too long, Hunter and Gretchen’s romance is definitely a highlight of the Billionaire series and I’m glad I read it. I’d recommend it for fans of her series that may have skipped this like I did or for those who just love variations on the Beauty and the Beast theme with hot romance and good banter. Read it. I’m glad I did.<br><br><br><br><br>For more reviews, visit<br><a href="http://afterdarkbooklovers.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453917680i/17891018.jpg" width="320" height="108" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/After-Dark-Book-Lovers/290327777811010?ref_type=bookmark" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453918230i/17891087.png" width="34" height="34" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/113109434312544905742/posts" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453918230i/17891089.png" width="34" height="34" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_677030362" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/677030362" />
    <a title="babyfishmouth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5107478-babyfishmouth"><img alt="babyfishmouth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1299881746p2/5107478.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/677030362?book_show_action=true">Jul 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="babyfishmouth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="babyfishmouth" href="/user/show/5107478-babyfishmouth">babyfishmouth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18242048-beauty-and-the-billionaire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5107478-babyfishmouth?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5107478-babyfishmouth?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer677030362" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2368346351272801495">I really disliked the first book in this series but I got lured into reading this one by the intriguing premise, low price and good reviews.<br/>I should have trusted my gut, though, and skipped it. <br/><br/>I love "Beauty and the Beast" stories but the execution on this one is poorly done. Hunter is a very reclusive 30 year old billionaire who overhears a three minute conversation between Gretchen and the heroine from the first book in the series. Somehow, in that brief amount of time, he concludes that Gret</span>
  <span id="freeText2368346351272801495" style="display:none">I really disliked the first book in this series but I got lured into reading this one by the intriguing premise, low price and good reviews.<br />I should have trusted my gut, though, and skipped it. <br /><br />I love "Beauty and the Beast" stories but the execution on this one is poorly done. Hunter is a very reclusive 30 year old billionaire who overhears a three minute conversation between Gretchen and the heroine from the first book in the series. Somehow, in that brief amount of time, he concludes that Gretchen is “bold and fearless” with a “smart mind and a sharp tongue” and she is meant to be with him. She begins to “haunt his dreams” and he declares that HE MUST HAVE HER. Because he’s so rich, he concocts a very expensive and ridiculous scheme to lure her into moving into his mansion for a month so he can be near her and win her heart. Once she’s in his mansion, though, he seems to forget all about his plan. He spends a lot of time getting angry with her, pushing her away and being a complete dick because he has scars (which are initially described as being on the left side of his face but two chapters later have miraculously migrated to the right side of his face). He firmly believes no one will ever love him because he’s so physically hideous. The “beauty and the beast” premise would have worked much better for me if he hadn’t been the one to orchestrate Gretchen moving into his house. His reluctance to enter into a relationship with Gretchen and rejection of all her advances would have seemed more organic and true if she had been unwillingly thrust into his life. Because he’s the catalyst, however, it seems like manufactured conflict to fill pages and build up sexual tension. Speaking of sexual tension, Hunter is a virgin and pretty damn pissy about it. Gretchen figures this out fairly early on and decides that she wants to enter into a relationship with him. She is drawn to his scars (of course) and wants to help him be less lonely. So what does she do? She barges in on him while he’s masturbating and gives him a blow job. Does Hunter figure out that this is pretty much a green light to proceed without caution with her? Nope. He continues to be surly and unreceptive to her flirting and sexual suggestions. Until suddenly he doesn’t and he becomes the aggressor. I found it all quite bewildering and hard to accept.<br /><br />As a result, I didn’t like Hunter at all. His speech is stiff and formal. He never uses contractions and says things like “Do you not like the quiet?” or “I simply wore a jacket because it was pleasing to me to dress well.” I think the author was trying to reinforce how uncomfortable he is around people but the dude wasn’t born in 1817 in London. He grew up in America in the 1990’s and went to Dartmouth College. His speech pattern should be that of a normal 30 year old guy. <br /><br />Gretchen is a lot more likable initially but then she takes a turn for the worse when she throws a dinner party to kick start Hunter back into society and force him out of his self-imposed exile. Once she became unlikable, I struggled to finish the book.<br /><br />Reading other reviews for this book, though, I seem to be in the minority as it has lots of 4 and 5 stars. It must be that Jessica Clare’s style of writing and storytelling isn’t for me. I’m not getting lured into reading the next book in the series no matter how tempting the premise and price.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2368346351272801495" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10640745151986547120">Summary <br/>Hunter Buchanan, is a real estate tycoon, and because he is scarred, no woman will come near him. He is respected because of his wealth and business intellect, but that is as far as it goes.   <span id="freeText10640745151986547120" style="display:none">Summary <br />Hunter Buchanan, is a real estate tycoon, and because he is scarred, no woman will come near him. He is respected because of his wealth and business intellect, but that is as far as it goes. He is lonely and craves companionship, and when he spies Gretchen he knows that she is the one woman for him. So he devises a plan to bring her to his home to work on some letters for writing a book, hoping to make her see the man beneath the scars. Gretchen is a ghostwriter, and when she is given a great offer to write and transcribe some letters for a new book, she can’t pass this opportunity up. When she arrives though, the mansion has only a few servants, and has a rigid schedule, and the man of the house is a recluse, and is a bit of a beast at times. But she senses more from Hunter than meets the eye, and despite his scars, she sees a man that needs her and she sees the man beneath his rough exterior, a man that has never known love or affection, and has only a few friends and one loyal bitter servant. Soon Hunter and Gretchen will soon learn that you need to have faith in love or it won’t work, will these two find a balance in each other?<br /><br />The Hero<br />Hunter Buchanan was kidnapped when he was a child, and trying to escape, ended up barely getting away alive, and was scarred for life. Hunter’s father was a man who cared more about money than his own son. But when Hunter went to college, the saving grace was the friends he made, friends that saw past his appearance and she the inner part of him. Hunter is a hero that is very “tortured male”…and it just broke my heart. It was quite heartbreaking seeing more and more of his character come through in this story, We see bits and pieces of him, a damaged man but not a broken one. He is on the hunt to be accepted and loved by a woman, to have passion and companionship. To be loved for who he is and not for his money.<br /><br />The Heroine <br />Gretchen is spirited and lively, and who wouldn’t love her. Gretchen makes a living by being a ghostwriter, but lately her writing has been falling short and she needs something more or she could be out on the streets soon. When she is given a offer, that is the best opportunity, but would have her living in a house with a man who is a recluse, she is cautious, but she is drawn to this opportunity. She soon sees that there is more to her boss than meets the eye, and sets out to show him who she really is. What I loved about Gretchen is her accepting nature, she doesn’t see Hunter as most others do, she sees a man hurting and in need of her. She takes a look at his scars, but doesn’t see a beast but a man worthy of love. Gretchen is bold and goes after her “prey” which was quite entertaining. I loved the way she goes after what she wants and is a fighter.<br /><br />Plot and Story Line <br />This is a “beauty and the beast” themed story but in a contemporary setting. Which I actually love this trope, and even though it can be overdone, I loved the way that Jessica Clare wrote this one. In the previous book, we see the beginning of the story happening, so it was fun seeing it just start off from where the first book left off. Beauty and the Billionaire, is a story that won my heart with every page written. I loved the different feel to this story from the first book. We have the Beauty (Gretchen), and the Beast (Hunter), and at first they don’t see much of each other, but Gretchen grows more bolder, and Hunter becomes more open to her advances, and it was quite entertaining seeing these two come together finally. There are quite a few obstacles that they need to overcome before they have any hope of getting their HEA, but they find it, and what a beautiful way it is found too. I love the flow of the story, and the writing just kept me reading and this was such a page turner, I had the most difficult time putting it down. This author has a talented way with her writing of captivating her audience. I found these two characters to be just wonderful for each other, and boy some of the bedroom scenes are quite thrilling and sexy, but what I loved most was seeing the love story to be the primary focus of the story, and seeing it grow and bloom was quite fun. Another great aspect was seeing the way this story comes together, it was very riveting at times, and kept me on tinder hooks, and it also gave us a little teaser at the end for the third book which I am very excited for now.<br /><br />The Cover<br />I still don’t know what to think about the covers. I mean they are pretty of course, but they aren’t really relevant to the story in any way.<br /><br />Overall View<br />Beauty and the Billioniare is an emotional love tale of compassion, trust, and what true love really takes….this is a story that is enthralls the reader with every page, a tender love story to capture you from page one. SIMPLY SPLENDID!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10640745151986547120" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7451210-amanda?shelf=handicap-scarred-hero">handicap-scarred-hero</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer728248627" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10741920138117751442">I always love a Beauty and the Beast theme book and will never miss reading one of it. I thought Book 1 Stranded with a Billionaire was good, but Book 2 Beauty and the Billionaire left me feeling slightly disappointed. The Hunter that I knew from Book 1 doesn't really live up to my expectation. Usually scarred hero can be insecure and vulnerable, but they will have another alpha side that make us swoon for them. However, that's really not the case here.<br/><br/>There is some flashback on previous book re</span>
  <span id="freeText10741920138117751442" style="display:none">I always love a Beauty and the Beast theme book and will never miss reading one of it. I thought Book 1 Stranded with a Billionaire was good, but Book 2 Beauty and the Billionaire left me feeling slightly disappointed. The Hunter that I knew from Book 1 doesn't really live up to my expectation. Usually scarred hero can be insecure and vulnerable, but they will have another alpha side that make us swoon for them. However, that's really not the case here.<br /><br />There is some flashback on previous book regarding Hunter's first meeting with Gretchen at an empty apartment. So if you didn't read book 1, you won't be missing out much. Just from that one encounter, Hunter is determined to have this woman that captivates him with her charm and tough exterior. I admire him for his determination, but found his way of trying to get to her slightly creepy. <br /><br />Gretchen, hmm... I totally like this girl from Book 1. She the elder sister of Audrey, Logan's assistant and working as a ghostwriter. She seems so tough, no-nonsense kinda girl, who loves adventure and gave some pretty good girl to girl advise to Bronte. But here, I found her simply too immature and irresponsible. Her career as a ghostwriter was a disaster, missing deadline and tons of procrastinating. I can't find myself sympathize with her when her landlord threaten to throw her on the street.<br /><br />So, Hunter offered a writing job to Gretchen that manage to keep her at his side that enable him to slowly work his way into her heart. However, instead of him working his way in, it seems that Gretchen is much fascinated with the grouchy and scarred owner of the mansion herself. Hunter is feeling elated, nervous and excited about this new development in his lonely life. <br /><br />What disappoint me is that Hunter is just simply too insecure with his disfigurement and never did any heroic moves that makes him worthy in my eyes. So I don't see why Gretchen keep giving him chances over and over again. I don't even understand the reason she like him. <br /><br />Logan, the hero from the previous book did make a little appearance, but there isn't much development between him and Bronte for us. When Hunter's relationship with Gretchen blew up in his face, he seek advice from Logan. But again, he is of no help at all. These guys should really stop asking each other for relationship advise. <br /><br />The next book is about Audrey, but I'm not sure which billionaire she is going to end up with. Reese, Cade, Griffin or Jonathan? I hope the next book is gonna be better. Finger crossed.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10741920138117751442" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText5865883111852884733" style="display:none">This story is sweet, romantic and hilarious all at the same time!! The 2nd book in the Billionaire boys club series....The story is about billionaire Hunter Buchanan &amp; ghost writer (who actually hates her occupation) Gretchen Petty. <br /><br />Incredibly lonely and physically scarred Hunter desperately wants to get to know the beautiful red-head Gretchen and goes to some, not so honest means, to do so. <br /><br />I felt so bad for Hunter and found myself feeling sorry for him. Having to sit in his big-ass dinning room in his big-ass manor house all alone....eating the hideous food prepared by Hunter's stuffy old butler Eldon. Gretchen ends up living in Hunter's house working for a new publishing company. Hired to read some very old letters found in a trunk, and write a story about them.<br /><br />Gretchen having a wonderful sense of humor, tries her best to get the, oh so serious Hunter to laugh and engage her in conversation. Slowly she break him out of the confines of his shell. Gretchen is the perfect match for Hunter, as she cares not about his terribly scarred face and only sees the hunky quiet man. Their relationship blossoms into a lovely romantic affair, though they do hit some bumps in the road along the way. <br /><br />Gretchen's hairless cat Igor is a nice addition to the cast of characters!!<br /><br />If you're looking for a funny, romantic, hot steamy read.....then this is the book for you!!         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1318008470" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9345459072832778398">Unapologetic, in your face, Beauty and the Beast story. And I'm a sucker for a good Beauty and the Beast story. There's a castle and roses and everything. This will be a re-read for me when I need a fun escape. Hunter Buchanan hides away from the world. He has some extensive scaring - and not cool scars like some romances but truly disfiguring scars - due to an incident in his childhood and has used this to keep everyone, even his few friends, from getting close. When he sees Gretchen, he forms </span>
  <span id="freeText9345459072832778398" style="display:none">Unapologetic, in your face, Beauty and the Beast story. And I'm a sucker for a good Beauty and the Beast story. There's a castle and roses and everything. This will be a re-read for me when I need a fun escape. Hunter Buchanan hides away from the world. He has some extensive scaring - and not cool scars like some romances but truly disfiguring scars - due to an incident in his childhood and has used this to keep everyone, even his few friends, from getting close. When he sees Gretchen, he forms a plan to get her in his life. He maps out carefully how he can slowly introduce himself to keep her from being horrified by his face. But Gretchen blows that out of the water leading to quiet a few funny moments. So what happens when you put a scarred, reclusive, desperately lonely 30 year old virgin and a blunt, sexually confident redhead together in a house for a month....I loved every word. <br /><br />I grant there are a few problems with this. Hunter really screws up, and the path back from that needed a bit more. I would have liked to have seen Gretchen and Hunter interact more outside of the tension. Honestly, I don't care about any of the writing issues. I just enjoyed this so much. </span>
  <a data-text-id="9345459072832778398" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('moiCOGJNVM22OnQlmOeoAsK5AJPFHeOXMHiHxWjChliGtxIuAxOLKGUh5mVS/qPH5pKRABG58hkmiy1XNV5S8A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('U2CBADPgHdC5p+FlXDqy6yIqARNjf4iKYSx0h+JgzHNPXxEWUr7CNWq8cyWWI7kuBgGQgLfbmQR3394Vv/wY2w==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText1414507322179662948" style="display:none">This is a pen name for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2923539.Jill_Myles" rel="nofollow noopener">Jill Myles</a>.<br /><br />Jill Myles has been an incurable romantic since childhood. She reads all the 'naughty parts' of books first, looks for a dirty joke in just about everything, and thinks to this day that the Little House on the Prairie books should have been steamier.<br /><br />After devouring hundreds of paperback romances, mythology books, and archaeological tomes, she decided to write a few books of her own - stories with a wild adventure, sharp banter, and lots of super-sexy situations. She prefers her heroes alpha and half-dressed, her heroines witty, and she loves nothing more than watching them overcome adversity to fall into bed together.</span>
